	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd') != 'fe3fbc3f360f29abcc610fbdb12d6a85c39451e4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd') !== 'fe3fbc3f360f29abcc610fbdb12d6a85c39451e4') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd') !== 'bc5eef214c884ed721ce755777337489b0b0da80') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/xml_schema.xsd') !== 'fe3fbc3f360f29abcc610fbdb12d6a85c39451e4') {
